building_ukn_foundry_4 = {
	base_buildtime = @building_ukn_foundry_6_build_time
	can_build = no
	position_priority = 121
	category = manufacturing

	potential = {
		NOR = {
			has_modifier = resort_colony
			has_modifier = slave_colony
		}
		UKN_USES_SUB_ALDERSON_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
		UKN_USES_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_EXTRACTION_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_RW_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_RW_EXTRACTION_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_RW_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_RW_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
	}

	allow = {
		has_upgraded_capital = yes
	}

	destroy_trigger = {
		OR = {
			UKN_USES_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_EXTRACTION_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_RW_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_RW_EXTRACTION_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_RW_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_RW_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_ALDERSON_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_ALDERSON_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_ALDERSON_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			has_modifier = resort_colony
			has_modifier = slave_colony
		}
	}


#[AI-DEFAULT] ==Force Build
	triggered_planet_modifier = {
		potential = {
			exists = owner
			owner = {
				is_ai = yes
				is_gestalt = no
			}
			NOT = { has_building = building_ukn_foundry_4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			job_foundry_add = 1000
		}
	}
#[AI-MACHINE] ==Force Build
	triggered_planet_modifier = {
		potential = {
			exists = owner
			owner = {
				is_ai = yes
				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_building = building_ukn_foundry_4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			job_fabricator_add = 1000
		}
	}
#[AI-MACHINE] ==Force Build
	triggered_planet_modifier = {
		potential = {
			exists = owner
			owner = {
				is_ai = yes
				is_hive_empire = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_building = building_ukn_foundry_4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			job_alloy_drone_add = 1000
		}
	}

building_ukn_factory_4 = {
	base_buildtime = @building_ukn_factory_6_build_time
	can_build = no
	position_priority = 122
	category = manufacturing

	potential = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			country_uses_consumer_goods = yes
		}
		NOR = {
			has_modifier = resort_colony
			has_modifier = slave_colony
		}
		UKN_USES_SUB_ALDERSON_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
		UKN_USES_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_EXTRACTION_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_RW_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_RW_EXTRACTION_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_RW_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_RW_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
	}

	allow = {
		has_upgraded_capital = yes
	}

	destroy_trigger = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			country_uses_consumer_goods = no
		}
		OR = {
			UKN_USES_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_EXTRACTION_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_RW_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_RW_EXTRACTION_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_RW_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_RW_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_ALDERSON_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_ALDERSON_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_ALDERSON_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			has_modifier = resort_colony
			has_modifier = slave_colony
		}
	}
	
	
#[AI-DEFAULT] ==Force Build
	triggered_planet_modifier = {
		potential = {
			exists = owner
			owner = {
				is_ai = yes
				is_gestalt = no
			}
			NOT = { has_building = building_ukn_factory_4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			job_artisan_add = 1000
		}
	}
#[AI-GESTALT] ==Force Build
	triggered_planet_modifier = {
		potential = {
			exists = owner
			owner = {
				is_ai = yes
				is_gestalt = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_building = building_ukn_factory_4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			job_artisan_drone_add = 1000
		}
	}
#----------------------------------------------------

	resources = {
		category = planet_buildings_ukn_factory_4
#########
# COSTS #
#########

		cost = {
			nanites = @building_ukn_factory_6_cost_basic_nanites
		}

			trigger = {

					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			consumer_goods = @building_ukn_factory_6_cost_basic_consumer_goods
		}
	
#[BASIC] MINERALS
		cost = {
			trigger = {
				exists = owner

	base_buildtime = @building_ukn_factory_7_build_time

		}
		NOR = {
			has_modifier = resort_colony
			has_modifier = slave_colony
		}
		UKN_USES_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_EXTRACTION_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_RW_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_RW_EXTRACTION_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_RW_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_RW_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_ALDERSON_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_ALDERSON_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
		UKN_USES_ALDERSON_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = no
	}

	allow = {
		has_upgraded_capital = yes
	}

			country_uses_consumer_goods = no

			UKN_USES_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes

			UKN_USES_RW_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes

			UKN_USES_ALDERSON_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			has_modifier = resort_colony
			has_modifier = slave_colony
		}
	}

	base_buildtime = @building_ukn_femtomatter_replication_grid_5_build_time

	potential = {
		NOR = {
			has_modifier = resort_colony

		has_upgraded_capital = yes

			UKN_USES_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_EXTRACTION_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes

			UKN_USES_MILITARY_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_RW_GAIA_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_RW_EXTRACTION_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
			UKN_USES_RW_SCIENCE_ARCOLOGY_DISTRICTS = yes
